See\\n1631:     :ref:`sphx_glr_auto_examples_developing_estimators_sklearn_is_fitted.py`\\n1632:     for an example on how to use the API.\\n1633: \\n1634:     If no `attributes` are passed, this function will pass if an estimator is stateless.\\n1635:     An estimator can indicate it's stateless by setting the `requires_fit` tag. See\\n1636:     :ref:`estimator_tags` for more information. Note that the `requires_fit` tag\\n1637:     is ignored if `attributes` are passed.\\n1638: \\n1639:     Parameters\\n1640:     ----------\\n1641:     estimator : estimator instance\\n1642:         Estimator instance for which the check is performed.\\n1643: \\n1644:     attributes : str, list or tuple of str, default=None\\n1645:         Attribute name(s) given as string or a list/tuple of strings\\n1646:         Eg.: ``[\\\"coef_\\\", \\\"estimator_\\\", ...], \\\"coef_\\\"``\\n1647: \\n1648:         If `None`, `estimator` is considered fitted if there exist an\\n1649:         attribute that ends with a underscore and does not start with double\\n1650:         underscore.\\n1651: \\n1652:     msg : str, default=None\\n1653:         The default error message is, \\\"This %(name)s instance is not fitted\\n1654:         yet.
